## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# CockroachDB Raft Consensus and Lease Management Cross-Component Discovery

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in cockroachdb/cockroach under pkg/kv/kvserver/ that implement the Raft consensus integration and range lease management. Identify: the Replica.handleRaftReady method and its state machine application, the Store.processReady batch processing, the lease request and transfer logic (RequestLease, TransferLease), the lease expiration vs epoch-based lease types, and the liveness-based node health checking that feeds into lease decisions. Report each file path and key function or type.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/cockroach--v24.3.0.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [

  ],

    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the CockroachDB repository's Raft consensus and lease management system. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've identified **34 source files** in `pkg/kv/kvserver/` that implement Raft consensus integration and range lease management:

### Key Components Discovered:

1. **Raft Consensus Pipeline**:
   - `Replica.handleRaftReady()` - Main entry point for Raft processing
   - `Replica.handleRaftReadyRaftMuLocked()` - Core Raft integration with etcd/raft library
   - `Store.processReady()` - Batch processing coordinator

2. **State Machine Application**:
   - `replicaStateMachine` - Implements apply.StateMachine interface
   - `replicaDecoder`, `replicatedCmd`, `replicaAppBatch` - Supporting components
   - Multi-stage application: prepare → batch → storage → side-effects

3. **Lease Management**:
   - `RequestLease()` and `TransferLease()` commands in batcheval package
   - `Replica.requestLeaseLocked()` for lease acquisition
   - `leases/build.go` and `leases/status.go` for lease construction and validation

4. **Lease Types**:
   - **Expiration-Based**: Absolute expiration timestamp, simple, frequent renewal
   - **Epoch-Based**: Bound to node liveness epochs, indefinite duration, heartbeat-based
   - **Leader Leases**: Tied to Raft leadership through leader fortification

5. **Liveness-Based Health Checking**:
   - `NodeLiveness` - Centralized failure detector with Heartbeat() and IncrementEpoch()
   - `Store.processTick()` - Integrates liveness map into Raft processing
   - `nodeIsLiveCallback()` - Updates liveness state and unquiesces ranges
   - Used by `leases/status.go` to determine epoch lease validity

    "content": "1: // Copyright 2016 The Cockroach Authors.\n2: //\n3: // Use of this software is governed by the CockroachDB Software License\n4: // included in the /LICENSE file.\n5: \n6: // This file contains replica methods related to range leases.\n7: //\n8: // Here be dragons: The lease system (especially for epoch-based\n9: // leases) relies on multiple interlocking conditional puts (here and\n10: // in NodeLiveness). This\n81: \t// includes calls to leaseStatus from the closed timestamp side-transport,\n82: \t// meaning that the following call to GetCurrentReadSummary is guaranteed to\n83: \t// observe the highest closed timestamp published under this lease.\n84: \t//\n85: \t// We perform this action during evaluation to ensure that the lease\n86: \t// revocation takes place regardless of whether the corresponding Raft\n87: \t// proposal succeeds, fails, or is ambiguous - in which case there's no\n88: \t// guarantee that the transfer will not still apply. Architecture\\n\\nThis analysis identifies all Go source files in `pkg/kv/kvserver/` that implement Raft consensus integration and range lease management in CockroachDB v24.3.0.\\n\\n## Core Raft Processing Pipeline\\n\\nThe Raft processing pipeline flows through:\\n\\n1. **Replica.handleRaftReady()** (`replica_raft.go:832`) - Entry point that acquires the raftMu lock and calls handleRaftReadyRaftMuLocked. This drives the main Raft loop by processing ready events from the Raft library.\\n\\n2. **Replica.handleRaftReadyRaftMuLocked()** (`replica_raft.go:867`) - Core Raft integration method that:\\n   - Takes incoming snapshots\\n   - Manages flow control levels (RACv1 to RACv2 transitions)\\n   - Integrates with etcd/raft library's RawNode\\n   - Handles message generation and log appending\\n   - Applies committed entries through the state machine\\n\\n3. **Store.processReady()** (`store_raft.go:671`) - Batch processing function that:\\n   - Looks up the replica by range ID\\n   - Calls handleRaftReady with CPU time tracking\\n   - Records metrics for Raft working duration and latency\\n\\n## Raft Scheduling\\n\\n**Scheduler.go** defines the Processor interface and its implementation that schedules:\\n- processReady() - for Raft ready events\\n- processTick() - for Raft heartbeat ticks with liveness map integration\\n- processRACv2PiggybackedAdmitted() - for flow control v2\\n\\n## State Machine Application\\n\\nThe state machine replication layer implements the `apply.StateMachine` interface through:\\n\\n1. **replicaStateMachine** (`replica_application_state_machine.go:58`) - Coordinates state transitions from committed Raft entries through multi-stage application:\\n   - Stage 1: Commands prepared in replicaAppBatch\\n   - Stage 2: Batch atomically committed to storage engine\\n   - Stage 3: Side-effects applied to in-memory state via ApplySideEffects()\\n\\n2. **replicaDecoder** (`replica_application_decoder.go`) - Implements apply.Decoder to decode committed Raft entries into replicatedCmd objects\\n\\n3. **replicatedCmd** (`replica_application_cmd.go`) - Implements apply.Command interfaces, storing state for applying individual Raft entries\\n\\n4. **replicaAppBatch** (`replica_app_batch.go`) - Implements apply.Batch with:\\n   - Stage() method for staging commands\\n   - ApplyToStateMachine() for flushing to storage engine\\n   - RocksDB batch accumulation for persistent state\\n\\n5. **Apply Package** (`apply/task.go`, `apply/cmd.go`) - Defines interfaces for state machine replication:\\n   - Command, CheckedCommand, AppliedCommand\\n   - Batch, EphemeralBatch\\n   - Task for coordinating entry application\\n\\n6. **CheckForcedErr** (`kvserverbase/forced_error.go`) - Determines if committed commands should be applied or rejected beneath Raft based on deterministic checks\\n\\n## Range Lease Management\\n\\n### Lease Request and Transfer Logic\\n\\n1. **Replica.requestLeaseLocked()** (`replica_range_lease.go:851`) - Initiates a lease acquisition or renewal:\\n   - Calls through the lease request pipeline\\n   - Respects quota limits on concurrent requests\\n   - Handles both expiration-based and epoch-based leases\\n\\n2. **RequestLease Command** (`batcheval/cmd_lease_request.go:48`) - Command evaluator that:\\n   - Verifies replica can receive the lease\\n   - Handles lease type switches (expiration to epoch promotion)\\n   - Manages previous lease revocation and expiration forwarding\\n   - No latches (non-MVCC) to avoid serializing with other requests\\n\\n3. **TransferLease Command** (`batcheval/cmd_lease_transfer.go:61`) - Transfers lease to another replica:\\n   - Allows overlap between old and new leases (unlike RequestLease)\\n   - Requires initiation by outgoing leaseholder\\n   - Declares all keys as latches (synchronizes with all requests)\\n   - Revokes previous lease before proposal to guarantee transfer\\n\\n### Lease Decision Logic\\n\\n1. **leases/build.go** - BuildInput and VerifyAndBuild() construct new leases:\\n   - Determines lease type (Expiration, Epoch, or Leader)\\n   - Handles heartbeat and epoch increment requirements for epoch leases\\n   - Validates against Raft snapshot requirements\\n\\n2. **leases/status.go** - Status() evaluates lease validity:\\n   - StatusInput provides current clock time and liveness information\\n   - Determines LeaseState (VALID, UNUSABLE, EXPIRED, PROSCRIBED)\\n   - For epoch leases: consults liveness record via NodeLiveness\\n   - For expiration leases: compares against lease.Expiration timestamp\\n\\n3. **leases/verify.go** - VerifyInput checks preconditions for lease changes\\n\\n### Lease Type Configuration\\n\\n**replica_range_lease.go** provides lease type selection:\\n\\n- **shouldUseExpirationLeaseRLocked()** - True if range should use expiration-based leases\\n- **requiresExpirationLeaseRLocked()** - True if NodeLiveness unavailable (meta/liveness ranges always use expiration)\\n- Settings control lease behavior:\\n  - ExpirationLeasesOnly - Forces all leases to expiration type\\n  - LeaderLeasesEnabled - Enables leader leases for Raft-fortified ranges\\n  - TransferExpirationLeasesFirstEnabled - Controls transfer of expiration vs epoch leases\\n\\n### Lease Expiration vs Epoch-Based Types\\n\\n**Expiration-Based Leases** (`LeaseExpiration`):\\n- Defined by absolute expiration timestamp\\n- Simple and fast but require frequent renewals\\n- Always used for meta and liveness ranges (no NodeLiveness dependency)\\n- Used as intermediate form in lease transfers\\n\\n**Epoch-Based Leases** (`LeaseEpoch`):\\n- Bound to node liveness epoch (heartbeat mechanism)\\n- Indefinite duration with periodic heartbeats\\n- Require epoch increment on node restart\\n- More efficient for stable ranges\\n- Depend on NodeLiveness for validity checking\\n\\n**Leader Leases** (`LeaseLeader`):\\n- Based on Raft leader term and support\\n- Used on ranges with Raft leader fortification\\n- Tied to Raft leadership through LeadSupportUntil\\n\\n## Liveness-Based Node Health Checking\\n\\n### NodeLiveness Integration\\n\\n1. **NodeLiveness** (`liveness/liveness.go:214`) - Centralized failure detector providing:\\n   - Heartbeat() - Node heartbeats to extend liveness expiration\\n   - IncrementEpoch() - Increments epoch when node resets/restarts\\n   - GetLiveness() and GetNodeVitalityFromCache() - Query liveness records\\n   - Verifies disk health before updating liveness (faulty disk = lose leases)\\n\\n2. **LivenessCache** (`liveness/cache.go`) - In-memory cache of liveness records:\\n   - Updated via gossip from liveness leaseholder\\n   - Tracks node liveness status for lease validity checks\\n   - Supports both direct liveness checks and store descriptor timestamps\\n\\n3. **IsLiveMap** (`liveness/livenesspb/liveness.go`) - Live node map:\\n   - Map of node liveness status for lease election\\n   - Updated through liveness change notifications\\n\\n### Feeding Liveness Into Lease Decisions\\n\\n1. **Store.processTick()** (`store_raft.go:696`) - Periodic processing:\\n   - Loads current livenessMap from store\\n   - Passes to replica.tick() for follower quiesce decisions\\n   - Calls nodeIsLiveCallback() on liveness changes\\n\\n2. **Store.nodeIsLiveCallback()** (`store_raft.go:731`) - Node liveness notifications:\\n   - Invoked when node transitions from non-live to live\\n   - Updates store's livenessMap\\n   - Unquiesces ranges where newly-live node is lagging replica\\n\\n3. **leases/status.go** - Status() uses NodeLiveness for epoch leases:\\n   - Calls nl.GetLiveness(lease.Replica.NodeID) to get liveness record\\n   - For epoch leases: compares lease.Epoch against liveness.Epoch\\n   - If epochs don't match or liveness unavailable, lease is EXPIRED\\n\\n4. **StorePool** (`allocator/storepool/store_pool.go:47`) - NodeLivenessFunc:\\n   - Provides MakeStorePoolNodeLivenessFunc()\\n   - Called with node ID to determine if node is live\\n   - Used by allocator for lease transfer target selection\\n\\n5. **Replica Store Liveness** (`replica_store_liveness.go`) - Per-replica liveness checks:\\n   - Integrates store liveness signals into replica operations\\n\\n## Related Files\\n\\n**Proposal and Quota Management**:\\n- `replica_proposal.go` - Command proposal with lease status logging\\n- `replica_proposal_buf.go` - Proposes batches through Raft\\n- `replica_proposal_quota.go` - Quota for lease and large requests\\n\\n**Raft Infrastructure**:\\n- `raft.go` - RawNode management and Raft transport\\n- `raft_log_truncator.go` - Raft log truncation orchestration\\n- `replica_raft_quiesce.go` - Range quiescing for idle ranges\\n- `replica_raft_overload.go` - Overload detection and handling\\n\\n**Metrics and Configuration**:\\n- `metrics.go` - Lease and Raft metrics (LeaseExpirationCount, LeaseEpochCount, LeaseLivenessCount)\\n- `testing_knobs.go` - Testing hooks for lease requests and transfers\\n\\n**Proto Definitions**:\\n- `kvserverpb/state.proto` - ReplicaState with RaftAppliedIndex and LeaseAppliedIndex\\n- `kvserverpb/lease_status.proto` - LeaseStatus and lease state machine\\n- `kvserverpb/proposer_kv.proto` - RaftCommand with IsLeaseRequest flag\\n\\n**Stores and Coordination**:\\n- `store.go` - Store-level management of replicas and metrics\\n- `replica.go` - Replica core state and checkLeaseRLocked()\\n- `storeliveness/` - Store liveness subsystem for detecting store health\\n\\nThis architecture ensures that:\\n1. Raft log entries are applied deterministically to the state machine\\n2. Lease validity depends on either absolute time or liveness-based epochs\\n3. Liveness health directly impacts lease validity and election decisions\\n4. Lease transfers use expiration-based intermediate forms for safety\\n5. Epoch-based leases provide efficient indefinite holding for stable ranges\\n\"\n}\n",

Processing Pipeline\\n\\nThe Raft processing pipeline flows through:\\n\\n1. **Replica.handleRaftReady()** (`replica_raft.go:832`) - Entry point that acquires the raftMu lock and calls handleRaftReadyRaftMuLocked. This drives the main Raft loop by processing ready events from the Raft library.\\n\\n2. **Replica.handleRaftReadyRaftMuLocked()** (`replica_raft.go:867`) - Core Raft integration method that:\\n   - Takes incoming snapshots\\n   - Manages flow control levels (RACv1 to RACv2 transitions)\\n   - Integrates with etcd/raft library's RawNode\\n   - Handles message generation and log appending\\n   - Applies committed entries through the state machine\\n\\n3. **Store.processReady()** (`store_raft.go:671`) - Batch processing function that:\\n   - Looks up the replica by range ID\\n   - Calls handleRaftReady with CPU time tracking\\n   - Records metrics for Raft working duration and latency\\n\\n## Raft Scheduling\\n\\n**Scheduler.go** defines the Processor interface and its implementation that schedules:\\n- processReady() - for Raft ready events\\n- processTick() - for Raft heartbeat ticks with liveness map integration\\n- processRACv2PiggybackedAdmitted() - for flow control v2\\n\\n## State Machine Application\\n\\nThe state machine replication layer implements the `apply.StateMachine` interface through:\\n\\n1. **replicaStateMachine** (`replica_application_state_machine.go:58`) - Coordinates state transitions from committed Raft entries through multi-stage application:\\n   - Stage 1: Commands prepared in replicaAppBatch\\n   - Stage 2: Batch atomically committed to storage engine\\n   - Stage 3: Side-effects applied to in-memory state via ApplySideEffects()\\n\\n2. **replicaDecoder** (`replica_application_decoder.go`) - Implements apply.Decoder to decode committed Raft entries into replicatedCmd objects\\n\\n3. **replicatedCmd** (`replica_application_cmd.go`) - Implements apply.Command interfaces, storing state for applying individual Raft entries\\n\\n4. **replicaAppBatch** (`replica_app_batch.go`) - Implements apply.Batch with:\\n   - Stage() method for staging commands\\n   - ApplyToStateMachine() for flushing to storage engine\\n   - RocksDB batch accumulation for persistent state\\n\\n5. **Apply Package** (`apply/task.go`, `apply/cmd.go`) - Defines interfaces for state machine replication:\\n   - Command, CheckedCommand, AppliedCommand\\n   - Batch, EphemeralBatch\\n   - Task for coordinating entry application\\n\\n6. **CheckForcedErr** (`kvserverbase/forced_error.go`) - Determines if committed commands should be applied or rejected beneath Raft based on deterministic checks\\n\\n## Range Lease Management\\n\\n### Lease Request and Transfer Logic\\n\\n1. **Replica.requestLeaseLocked()** (`replica_range_lease.go:851`) - Initiates a lease acquisition or renewal:\\n   - Calls through the lease request pipeline\\n   - Respects quota limits on concurrent requests\\n   - Handles both expiration-based and epoch-based leases\\n\\n2. **RequestLease Command** (`batcheval/cmd_lease_request.go:48`) - Command evaluator that:\\n   - Verifies replica can receive the lease\\n   - Handles lease type switches (expiration to epoch promotion)\\n   - Manages previous lease revocation and expiration forwarding\\n   - No latches (non-MVCC) to avoid serializing with other requests\\n\\n3. **TransferLease Command** (`batcheval/cmd_lease_transfer.go:61`) - Transfers lease to another replica:\\n   - Allows overlap between old and new leases (unlike RequestLease)\\n   - Requires initiation by outgoing leaseholder\\n   - Declares all keys as latches (synchronizes with all requests)\\n   - Revokes previous lease before proposal to guarantee transfer\\n\\n### Lease Decision Logic\\n\\n1. **leases/build.go** - BuildInput and VerifyAndBuild() construct new leases:\\n   - Determines lease type (Expiration, Epoch, or Leader)\\n   - Handles heartbeat and epoch increment requirements for epoch leases\\n   - Validates against Raft snapshot requirements\\n\\n2. **leases/status.go** - Status() evaluates lease validity:\\n   - StatusInput provides current clock time and liveness information\\n   - Determines LeaseState (VALID, UNUSABLE, EXPIRED, PROSCRIBED)\\n   - For epoch leases: consults liveness record via NodeLiveness\\n   - True if range should use expiration-based leases\\n- **requiresExpirationLeaseRLocked()** - True if NodeLiveness unavailable (meta/liveness ranges always use expiration)\\n- Settings control lease behavior:\\n  - ExpirationLeasesOnly - Forces all leases to expiration type\\n  - LeaderLeasesEnabled - Enables leader leases for Raft-fortified ranges\\n  - TransferExpirationLeasesFirstEnabled - Controls transfer of expiration vs epoch leases\\n\\n### Lease Expiration vs Epoch-Based Types\\n\\n**Expiration-Based Leases** (`LeaseExpiration`):\\n- Defined by absolute expiration timestamp\\n- Simple and fast but require frequent renewals\\n- Always used for meta and liveness ranges (no NodeLiveness dependency)\\n- Used as intermediate form in lease transfers\\n\\n**Epoch-Based Leases** (`LeaseEpoch`):\\n- Bound to node liveness epoch (heartbeat mechanism)\\n- Indefinite duration with periodic heartbeats\\n- Require epoch increment on node restart\\n- More efficient for stable ranges\\n- Depend on NodeLiveness for validity checking\\n\\n**Leader Leases** (`LeaseLeader`):\\n- Based on Raft leader term and support\\n- Used on ranges with Raft leader fortification\\n- Tied to Raft leadership through LeadSupportUntil\\n\\n## Liveness-Based Node Health Checking\\n\\n### NodeLiveness Integration\\n\\n1. **NodeLiveness** (`liveness/liveness.go:214`) - Centralized failure detector providing:\\n   - Heartbeat() - Node heartbeats to extend liveness expiration\\n   - IncrementEpoch() - Increments epoch when node resets/restarts\\n   - GetLiveness() and GetNodeVitalityFromCache() - Query liveness records\\n   - Verifies disk health before updating liveness (faulty disk = lose leases)\\n\\n2. **LivenessCache** (`liveness/cache.go`) - In-memory cache of liveness records:\\n   - Updated via gossip from liveness leaseholder\\n   - Tracks node liveness status for lease validity checks\\n   - Supports both direct liveness checks and store descriptor timestamps\\n\\n3. **IsLiveMap** (`liveness/livenesspb/liveness.go`) - Live node map:\\n   - Map of node liveness status for lease election\\n   - Updated through liveness change notifications\\n\\n### Feeding Liveness Into Lease Decisions\\n\\n1. **Store.processTick()** (`store_raft.go:696`) - Periodic processing:\\n   - Loads current livenessMap from store\\n   - Passes to replica.tick() for follower quiesce decisions\\n   - Calls nodeIsLiveCallback() on liveness changes\\n\\n2. **Store.nodeIsLiveCallback()** (`store_raft.go:731`) - Node liveness notifications:\\n   - Invoked when node transitions from non-live to live\\n   - Updates store's livenessMap\\n   - Unquiesces ranges where newly-live node is lagging replica\\n\\n3. **leases/status.go** - Status() uses NodeLiveness for epoch leases:\\n   - Calls nl.GetLiveness(lease.Replica.NodeID) to get liveness record\\n   - For epoch leases: compares lease.Epoch against liveness.Epoch\\n   - If epochs don't match or liveness unavailable, lease is EXPIRED\\n\\n4. **StorePool** (`allocator/storepool/store_pool.go:47`) - NodeLivenessFunc:\\n   - Provides MakeStorePoolNodeLivenessFunc()\\n   - Called with node ID to determine if node is live\\n   - Used by allocator for lease transfer target selection\\n\\n5. **Replica Store Liveness** (`replica_store_liveness.go`) - Per-replica liveness checks:\\n   - Integrates store liveness signals into replica operations\\n\\n## Related Files\\n\\n**Proposal and Quota Management**:\\n- `replica_proposal.go` - Command proposal with lease status logging\\n- `replica_proposal_buf.go` - Proposes batches through Raft\\n- `replica_proposal_quota.go` - Quota for lease and large requests\\n\\n**Raft Infrastructure**:\\n- `raft.go` - RawNode management and Raft transport\\n- `raft_log_truncator.go` - Raft log truncation orchestration\\n- `replica_raft_quiesce.go` - Range quiescing for idle ranges\\n- `replica_raft_overload.go` - Overload detection and handling\\n\\n**Metrics and Configuration**:\\n- `metrics.go` - Lease and Raft metrics (LeaseExpirationCount, LeaseEpochCount, LeaseLivenessCount)\\n- `testing_knobs.go` - Testing hooks for lease requests and transfers\\n\\n**Proto Definitions**:\\n- `kvserverpb/state.proto` - ReplicaState with RaftAppliedIndex and LeaseAppliedIndex\\n- `kvserverpb/lease_status.proto` - LeaseStatus and lease state machine\\n- `kvserverpb/proposer_kv.proto` - RaftCommand with IsLeaseRequest flag\\n\\n**Stores and Coordination**:\\n- `store.go` - Raft log entries are applied deterministically to the state machine\\n2. Lease validity depends on either absolute time or liveness-based epochs\\n3. Liveness health directly impacts lease validity and election decisions\\n4. Lease transfers use expiration-based intermediate forms for safety\\n5.
